SDL_Renderer

SDL_Renderer structure defines one SDL2 re= nderer. Assumptions used directly SDL2 compiled SDK words. We can not see i= ts internal structure.

Definition of it in the header file has only o= ne line of code. For example, you see.

/**
 * \brief A structure representing rendering state
 */
struct SDL_Renderer;
typedef struct SDL_Renderer SDL_Renderer;

Source project can be= seen in the definition SDL_Renderer located render\SDL_sysrender.h file.

For example, its definition.

The follow= ing look at how to create this SDL_Renderer.


SDL_CreateRenderer(= )

Function brief

SDL renderer to create a form b= ased on the use of SDL_CreateRenderer (). SDL_CreateRenderer () Prototype e= .g. less.
SDL_Renderer * SDLCALL SDL_CreateRenderer(SDL_Window * window,
                                               int index, Uint32 flags);
Parameters such as the following meanings.
window: renderin=
g the target form.
index: Index intends to initialize rendering devic=
es.
Set "-1" is the default rendering device initialization.
fl=
ags: supports the following values (in SDL_RendererFlags definition)
&nb=
sp;   SDL_RENDERER_SOFTWARE: Use software rendering
   =
; SDL_RENDERER_ACCELERATED: Use hardware acceleration
    SDL_=
RENDERER_PRESENTVSYNC: synchronization and refresh rate of the display
<=
p>    SDL_RENDERER_TARGETTEXTURE: do not understand
Return =
is created renderer's ID. Suppose you create a failure NULL is returned.

Source code analysis

SDL_CreateR= enderer () source positioned render\SDL_render.c in, for example, see.

<= pre code_snippet_id=3D"" snippet_file_name=3D"" name=3D"" class=3D"">SDL_Re= nderer * SDL_CreateRenderer(SDL_Window * window, int index, Uint32 flags) { #if !SDL_RENDER_DISABLED SDL_Renderer *renderer =3D NULL; int n =3D SDL_GetNumRenderDrivers(); const char *hint; if (!window) { SDL_SetError("Invalid window"); return NULL; } if (SDL_GetRenderer(window)) { SDL_SetError("Renderer already associated with window"); return NULL; } hint =3D SDL_GetHint(SDL_HINT_RENDER_VSYNC); if (hint) { if (*hint =3D=3D '0') { flags &=3D ~SDL_RENDERER_PRESENTVSYNC; } else { flags |=3D SDL_RENDERER_PRESENTVSYNC; } } if (index < 0) { hint =3D SDL_GetHint(SDL_HINT_RENDER_DRIVER); if (hint) { for (index =3D 0; index < n; ++index) { const SDL_RenderDriver *driver =3D render_drivers[index]; if (SDL_strcasecmp(hint, driver->info.name) =3D=3D 0) { /* Create a new renderer instance */ renderer =3D driver->CreateRenderer(window, flags); break; } } } if (!renderer) { for (index =3D 0; index < n; ++index) { const SDL_RenderDriver *driver =3D render_drivers[index]; if ((driver->info.flags & flags) =3D=3D flags) { /* Create a new renderer instance */ renderer =3D driver->CreateRenderer(window, flags); if (renderer) { /* Yay, we got one! */ break; } } } } if (index =3D=3D n) { SDL_SetError("Couldn't find matching render driver"); return NULL; } } else { if (index >=3D SDL_GetNumRenderDrivers()) { SDL_SetError("index must be -1 or in the range of 0 - %d", SDL_GetNumRenderDrivers() - 1); return NULL; } /* Create a new renderer instance */ renderer =3D render_drivers[index]->CreateRenderer(window, flags= ); } if (renderer) { renderer->magic =3D &renderer_magic; renderer->window =3D window; renderer->scale.x =3D 1.0f; renderer->scale.y =3D 1.0f; if (SDL_GetWindowFlags(window) & (SDL_WINDOW_HIDDEN|SDL_WINDOW_= MINIMIZED)) { renderer->hidden =3D SDL_TRUE; } else { renderer->hidden =3D SDL_FALSE; } SDL_SetWindowData(window, SDL_WINDOWRENDERDATA, renderer); SDL_RenderSetViewport(renderer, NULL); SDL_AddEventWatch(SDL_RendererEventWatch, renderer); SDL_LogInfo(SDL_LOG_CATEGORY_RENDER, "Created renderer: %s", renderer->info.name); } return renderer; #else SDL_SetError("SDL not built with rendering support"); return NULL; #endif }
SDL_CreateRenderer () is the most important function is that it = calls SDL_RenderDriver of CreateRenderer () method. The ability to create a= renderer by this method.

Surrounded by this method, comprising a number = of initialization and some finishing work.

The following were analyze= d for this core function.
We first look at SDL_RenderDriver this struct= ure. As can be seen from the literal meaning it represents a "driver render= er."

This structure is defined in the following example.

/* Define the =
SDL render driver structure */
struct SDL_RenderDriver
{
    SDL_Renderer *(*CreateRenderer) (SDL_Window * window, Uint32 flags);


   /* Info about the renderer capabilities */
    SDL_RendererInfo info;
};

As can be seen from the code, members of this structure is rela= tively simple. It includes a function pointer createRenderer () and a struc= ture of a type info SDL_RendererInfo storing information. CreateRenderer ()= is a function for creating a renderer, and is SDL_RendererInfo includes so= me information of the structure. Be able to look at the definition of SDL_R= endererInfo.
/**
 * \brief Information on the capabilities of a render driver or context.
 */
typedef struct SDL_RendererInfo
{
    const char *name;          /**< The name of the renderer */
    Uint32 flags;              /**< Supported ::SDL_RendererFlags */
    Uint32 num_texture_formats;/**< The number of available texture form=
ats */
    Uint32 texture_formats[16];/**< The available texture formats */
    int max_texture_width;     /**< The maximimum texture width */
    int max_texture_height;    /**< The maximimum texture height */
} SDL_RendererInfo;

There is a global SDL_RenderDriver types of st= atic arrays render_drivers in the SDL, which SDL stores all supported rende= rer.

For example, the array is defined.

static const SDL_RenderDriver *=

    &PSP_RenderDriver,

    &SW_RenderDriver

This structure related SDL_RenderDriver not say an= y more. The following are a look at the method of creating Direct3D, OpenGL= , Software three most common renderer.

1.Direct3D

Direct3D re= nderer creating function is D3D_CreateRenderer (). This function is located= render\direct3d\SDL_render_d3d.c file. First look at its code.

SDL_Renderer =
* D3D_CreateRenderer(SDL_Window * window, Uint32 flags)
{
    SDL_Renderer *renderer;
    D3D_RenderData *data;
    SDL_SysWMinfo windowinfo;
    HRESULT result;
    const char *hint;
    D3DPRESENT_PARAMETERS pparams;
    IDirect3DSwapChain9 *chain;
    D3DCAPS9 caps;
    DWORD device_flags;
    Uint32 window_flags;
    int w, h;
    SDL_DisplayMode fullscreen_mode;
    int displayIndex;


    renderer =3D (SDL_Renderer *) SDL_calloc(1, sizeof(*renderer));
    if (!renderer) {
        SDL_OutOfMemory();
        return NULL;
    }


    data =3D (D3D_RenderData *) SDL_calloc(1, sizeof(*data));
    if (!data) {
        SDL_free(renderer);
        SDL_OutOfMemory();
        return NULL;
    }


    if (!D3D_LoadDLL(&data->d3dDLL, &data->d3d)) {
        SDL_free(renderer);
        SDL_free(data);
        SDL_SetError("Unable to create Direct3D interface");
        return NULL;
    }


    renderer->WindowEvent =3D D3D_WindowEvent;
    renderer->CreateTexture =3D D3D_CreateTexture;
    renderer->UpdateTexture =3D D3D_UpdateTexture;
    renderer->UpdateTextureYUV =3D D3D_UpdateTextureYUV;
    renderer->LockTexture =3D D3D_LockTexture;
    renderer->UnlockTexture =3D D3D_UnlockTexture;
    renderer->SetRenderTarget =3D D3D_SetRenderTarget;
    renderer->UpdateViewport =3D D3D_UpdateViewport;
    renderer->UpdateClipRect =3D D3D_UpdateClipRect;
    renderer->RenderClear =3D D3D_RenderClear;
    renderer->RenderDrawPoints =3D D3D_RenderDrawPoints;
    renderer->RenderDrawLines =3D D3D_RenderDrawLines;
    renderer->RenderFillRects =3D D3D_RenderFillRects;
    renderer->RenderCopy =3D D3D_RenderCopy;
    renderer->RenderCopyEx =3D D3D_RenderCopyEx;
    renderer->RenderReadPixels =3D D3D_RenderReadPixels;
    renderer->RenderPresent =3D D3D_RenderPresent;
    renderer->DestroyTexture =3D D3D_DestroyTexture;
    renderer->DestroyRenderer =3D D3D_DestroyRenderer;
    renderer->info =3D D3D_RenderDriver.info;
    renderer->info.flags =3D (SDL_RENDERER_ACCELERATED | SDL_RENDERER_TA=
RGETTEXTURE);
    renderer->driverdata =3D data;


    SDL_VERSION(&windowinfo.version);
    SDL_GetWindowWMInfo(window, &windowinfo);


    window_flags =3D SDL_GetWindowFlags(window);
    SDL_GetWindowSize(window, &w, &h);
    SDL_GetWindowDisplayMode(window, &fullscreen_mode);


    SDL_zero(pparams);
    pparams.hDeviceWindow =3D windowinfo.info.win.window;
    pparams.BackBufferWidth =3D w;
    pparams.BackBufferHeight =3D h;
    if (window_flags & SDL_WINDOW_FULLSCREEN) {
        pparams.BackBufferFormat =3D
            PixelFormatToD3DFMT(fullscreen_mode.format);
    } else {
        pparams.BackBufferFormat =3D D3DFMT_UNKNOWN;
    }
    pparams.BackBufferCount =3D 1;
    pparams.SwapEffect =3D D3DSWAPEFFECT_DISCARD;


    if (window_flags & SDL_WINDOW_FULLSCREEN) {
        if ((window_flags & SDL_WINDOW_FULLSCREEN_DESKTOP) =3D=3D SDL_W=
INDOW_FULLSCREEN_DESKTOP)  {
            pparams.Windowed =3D TRUE;
            pparams.FullScreen_RefreshRateInHz =3D 0;
        } else {
            pparams.Windowed =3D FALSE;
            pparams.FullScreen_RefreshRateInHz =3D fullscreen_mode.refresh_=
rate;
        }
    } else {
        pparams.Windowed =3D TRUE;
        pparams.FullScreen_RefreshRateInHz =3D 0;
    }
    if (flags & SDL_RENDERER_PRESENTVSYNC) {
        pparams.PresentationInterval =3D D3DPRESENT_INTERVAL_ONE;
    } else {
        pparams.PresentationInterval =3D D3DPRESENT_INTERVAL_IMMEDIATE;
    }


   /* Get the adapter for the display that the window is on */
    displayIndex =3D SDL_GetWindowDisplayIndex(window);
    data->adapter =3D SDL_Direct3D9GetAdapterIndex(displayIndex);


    IDirect3D9_GetDeviceCaps(data->d3d, data->adapter, D3DDEVTYPE_HAL=
, &caps);


    device_flags =3D D3DCREATE_FPU_PRESERVE;
    if (caps.DevCaps & D3DDEVCAPS_HWTRANSFORMANDLIGHT) {
        device_flags |=3D D3DCREATE_HARDWARE_VERTEXPROCESSING;
    } else {
        device_flags |=3D D3DCREATE_SOFTWARE_VERTEXPROCESSING;
    }


    hint =3D SDL_GetHint(SDL_HINT_RENDER_DIRECT3D_THREADSAFE);
    if (hint && SDL_atoi(hint)) {
        device_flags |=3D D3DCREATE_MULTITHREADED;
    }


    result =3D IDirect3D9_CreateDevice(data->d3d, data->adapter,
                                     D3DDEVTYPE_HAL,
                                     pparams.hDeviceWindow,
                                     device_flags,
                                     &pparams, &data->device);
    if (FAILED(result)) {
        D3D_DestroyRenderer(renderer);
        D3D_SetError("CreateDevice()", result);
        return NULL;
    }


   /* Get presentation parameters to fill info */
    result =3D IDirect3DDevice9_GetSwapChain(data->device, 0, &chain=
);
    if (FAILED(result)) {
        D3D_DestroyRenderer(renderer);
        D3D_SetError("GetSwapChain()", result);
        return NULL;
    }
    result =3D IDirect3DSwapChain9_GetPresentParameters(chain, &pparams=
);
    if (FAILED(result)) {
        IDirect3DSwapChain9_Release(chain);
        D3D_DestroyRenderer(renderer);
        D3D_SetError("GetPresentParameters()", result);
        return NULL;
    }
    IDirect3DSwapChain9_Release(chain);
    if (pparams.PresentationInterval =3D=3D D3DPRESENT_INTERVAL_ONE) {
        renderer->info.flags |=3D SDL_RENDERER_PRESENTVSYNC;
    }
    data->pparams =3D pparams;


    IDirect3DDevice9_GetDeviceCaps(data->device, &caps);
    renderer->info.max_texture_width =3D caps.MaxTextureWidth;
    renderer->info.max_texture_height =3D caps.MaxTextureHeight;
    if (caps.NumSimultaneousRTs >=3D 2) {
        renderer->info.flags |=3D SDL_RENDERER_TARGETTEXTURE;
    }


    if (caps.PrimitiveMiscCaps & D3DPMISCCAPS_SEPARATEALPHABLEND) {
        data->enableSeparateAlphaBlend =3D SDL_TRUE;
    }


   /* Store the default render target */
    IDirect3DDevice9_GetRenderTarget(data->device, 0, &data->defa=
ultRenderTarget );
    data->currentRenderTarget =3D NULL;


   /* Set up parameters for rendering */
    D3D_InitRenderState(data);


    if (caps.MaxSimultaneousTextures >=3D 3)
    {
#ifdef ASSEMBLE_SHADER
       /* This shader was created by running the following HLSL through the=
 fxc compiler
           and then tuning the generated assembly.


           fxc/T fx_4_0/O3/Gfa/Fc yuv.fxc yuv.fx


           --- yuv.fx ---
           Texture2D g_txY;
           Texture2D g_txU;
           Texture2D g_txV;


           SamplerState samLinear
           {
               Filter =3D ANISOTROPIC;
               AddressU =3D Clamp;
               AddressV =3D Clamp;
               MaxAnisotropy =3D 1;
           };


           struct VS_OUTPUT
           {
                float2 TextureUV  : TEXCOORD0;
           };


           struct PS_OUTPUT
           {
                float4 RGBAColor : SV_Target;
           };


           PS_OUTPUT YUV420( VS_OUTPUT In )=20
           {
               const float3 offset =3D {-0.0625, -0.5, -0.5};
               const float3 Rcoeff =3D {1.164,  0.000,  1.596};
               const float3 Gcoeff =3D {1.164, -0.391, -0.813};
               const float3 Bcoeff =3D {1.164,  2.018,  0.000};


               PS_OUTPUT Output;
               float2 TextureUV =3D In.TextureUV;


               float3 yuv;
               yuv.x =3D g_txY.Sample( samLinear, TextureUV ).r;
               yuv.y =3D g_txU.Sample( samLinear, TextureUV ).r;
               yuv.z =3D g_txV.Sample( samLinear, TextureUV ).r;


               yuv +=3D offset;
               Output.RGBAColor.r =3D dot(yuv, Rcoeff);
               Output.RGBAColor.g =3D dot(yuv, Gcoeff);
               Output.RGBAColor.b =3D dot(yuv, Bcoeff);
               Output.RGBAColor.a =3D 1.0f;


               return Output;
           }


           technique10 RenderYUV420
           {
               pass P0
               {
                    SetPixelShader( CompileShader( ps_4_0_level_9_0, YUV420=
() ) );
               }
           }
        */
        const char *shader_text =3D
            "ps_2_0\n"
            "def c0, -0.0625, -0.5, -0.5, 1\n"
            "def c1, 1.16400003, 0, 1.59599996, 0\n"
            "def c2, 1.16400003, -0.391000003, -0.813000023, 0\n"
            "def c3, 1.16400003, 2.01799989, 0, 0\n"
            "dcl t0.xy\n"
            "dcl v0.xyzw\n"
            "dcl_2d s0\n"
            "dcl_2d s1\n"
            "dcl_2d s2\n"
            "texld r0, t0, s0\n"
            "texld r1, t0, s1\n"
            "texld r2, t0, s2\n"
            "mov r0.y, r1.x\n"
            "mov r0.z, r2.x\n"
            "add r0.xyz, r0, c0\n"
            "dp3 r1.x, r0, c1\n"
            "dp3 r1.y, r0, c2\n"
            "dp2add r1.z, r0, c3, c3.z\n"  /* Logically this is "dp3 r1.z, =
r0, c3" but the optimizer did its magic */
            "mov r1.w, c0.w\n"
            "mul r0, r1, v0\n"             /* Not in the HLSL, multiply by =
vertex color */
            "mov oC0, r0\n"
        ;
        LPD3DXBUFFER pCode;
        LPD3DXBUFFER pErrorMsgs;
        LPDWORD shader_data =3D NULL;
        DWORD   shader_size =3D 0;
        result =3D D3DXAssembleShader(shader_text, SDL_strlen(shader_text),=
 NULL, NULL, 0, &pCode, &pErrorMsgs);
        if (!FAILED(result)) {
            shader_data =3D (DWORD*)pCode->lpVtbl->GetBufferPointer(p=
Code);
            shader_size =3D pCode->lpVtbl->GetBufferSize(pCode);
            PrintShaderData(shader_data, shader_size);
        } else {
            const char *error =3D (const char *)pErrorMsgs->lpVtbl->G=
etBufferPointer(pErrorMsgs);
            SDL_SetError("Couldn't assemble shader: %s", error);
        }
#else
        const DWORD shader_data[] =3D {
            0xffff0200, 0x05000051, 0xa00f0000, 0xbd800000, 0xbf000000, 0xb=
f000000,
            0x3f800000, 0x05000051, 0xa00f0001, 0x3f94fdf4, 0x00000000, 0x3=
fcc49ba,
            0x00000000, 0x05000051, 0xa00f0002, 0x3f94fdf4, 0xbec83127, 0xb=
f5020c5,
            0x00000000, 0x05000051, 0xa00f0003, 0x3f94fdf4, 0x400126e9, 0x0=
0000000,
            0x00000000, 0x0200001f, 0x80000000, 0xb0030000, 0x0200001f, 0x8=
0000000,
            0x900f0000, 0x0200001f, 0x90000000, 0xa00f0800, 0x0200001f, 0x9=

            0x03000042, 0x800f0002, 0xb0e40000, 0xa0e40802, 0x02000001, 0x8=

            0x80000001, 0x02000001, 0x80040000, 0x80000002, 0x03000002, 0x8=

            0x80e40000, 0xa0e40000, 0x03000008, 0x80010001, 0x80e40000, 0xa=

            0x03000008, 0x80020001, 0x80e40000, 0xa0e40002, 0x0400005a, 0x8=

        if (shader_data !=3D NULL) {
            result =3D IDirect3DDevice9_CreatePixelShader(data->device, =
shader_data, &data->ps_yuv);
            if (!FAILED(result)) {
                renderer->info.texture_formats[renderer->info.num_tex=

                renderer->info.texture_formats[renderer->info.num_tex=
ture_formats++] =3D SDL_PIXELFORMAT_IYUV;
            } else {

    }


    return renderer;
}

(2) Loading Direct3D
Loadin= g completed by Direct3D function D3D_LoadDLL ().

Calling the function= IDirect3D9 possible to obtain a type of interface. IDirect3D9 interfaces c= an be used to complete the initial work D3D perhaps.

Code D3D_LoadDLL= () function in the following example.

SDL_bool D3D_LoadDLL( void **pD3DD=
LL, IDirect3D9 **pDirect3D9Interface )
{
	*pD3DDLL =3D SDL_LoadObject("D3D9.DLL");
	if (*pD3DDLL) {
		IDirect3D9 *(WINAPI * D3DCreate) (UINT SDKVersion);


		D3DCreate =3D
			(IDirect3D9 * (WINAPI *) (UINT)) SDL_LoadFunction(*pD3DDLL,
			"Direct3DCreate9");
		if (D3DCreate) {
			*pDirect3D9Interface =3D D3DCreate(D3D_SDK_VERSION);
		}
		if (!*pDirect3D9Interface) {
			SDL_UnloadObject(*pD3DDLL);
			*pD3DDLL =3D NULL;
			return SDL_FALSE;
		}


		return SDL_TRUE;
	} else {
		*pDirect3D9Interface =3D NULL;
		return SDL_FALSE;
	}
}

As can be seen from the code, the function is loaded a "D3D9.DLL= " the Dll. And it called among Direct3DCreate9 () method.

= (4) Creating Device

<= p>(5) set the rendering state

Rendering state in the fu= nction setting is completed D3D_InitRenderState () in. This knowledge is no= longer part of the detailed description, reference can be related Direct3D= rendering tutorial. Posted D3D_InitRenderState () code.
static void D3D_Init=
RenderState(D3D_RenderData *data)
{
    D3DMATRIX matrix;


    IDirect3DDevice9 *device =3D data->device;


    IDirect3DDevice9_SetVertexShader(device, NULL);
    IDirect3DDevice9_SetFVF(device, D3DFVF_XYZ | D3DFVF_DIFFUSE | D3DFVF_TE=
X1);
    IDirect3DDevice9_SetRenderState(device, D3DRS_ZENABLE, D3DZB_FALSE);
    IDirect3DDevice9_SetRenderState(device, D3DRS_CULLMODE, D3DCULL_NONE);
    IDirect3DDevice9_SetRenderState(device, D3DRS_LIGHTING, FALSE);


   /* Enable color modulation by diffuse color */
    IDirect3DDevice9_SetTextureStageState(device, 0, D3DTSS_COLOROP,
                                          D3DTOP_MODULATE);
    IDirect3DDevice9_SetTextureStageState(device, 0, D3DTSS_COLORARG1,
                                          D3DTA_TEXTURE);
    IDirect3DDevice9_SetTextureStageState(device, 0, D3DTSS_COLORARG2,
                                          D3DTA_DIFFUSE);


   /* Enable alpha modulation by diffuse alpha */
    IDirect3DDevice9_SetTextureStageState(device, 0, D3DTSS_ALPHAOP,
                                          D3DTOP_MODULATE);
    IDirect3DDevice9_SetTextureStageState(device, 0, D3DTSS_ALPHAARG1,
                                          D3DTA_TEXTURE);
    IDirect3DDevice9_SetTextureStageState(device, 0, D3DTSS_ALPHAARG2,
                                          D3DTA_DIFFUSE);


   /* Enable separate alpha blend function, if possible */
    if (data->enableSeparateAlphaBlend) {
        IDirect3DDevice9_SetRenderState(device, D3DRS_SEPARATEALPHABLENDENA=
BLE, TRUE);
    }


   /* Disable second texture stage, since we're done */
    IDirect3DDevice9_SetTextureStageState(device, 1, D3DTSS_COLOROP,
                                          D3DTOP_DISABLE);
    IDirect3DDevice9_SetTextureStageState(device, 1, D3DTSS_ALPHAOP,
                                          D3DTOP_DISABLE);


   /* Set an identity world and view matrix */
    matrix.m[0][0] =3D 1.0f;
    matrix.m[0][1] =3D 0.0f;
    matrix.m[0][2] =3D 0.0f;
    matrix.m[0][3] =3D 0.0f;
    matrix.m[1][0] =3D 0.0f;
    matrix.m[1][1] =3D 1.0f;
    matrix.m[1][2] =3D 0.0f;
    matrix.m[1][3] =3D 0.0f;
    matrix.m[2][0] =3D 0.0f;
    matrix.m[2][1] =3D 0.0f;
    matrix.m[2][2] =3D 1.0f;
    matrix.m[2][3] =3D 0.0f;
    matrix.m[3][0] =3D 0.0f;
    matrix.m[3][1] =3D 0.0f;
    matrix.m[3][2] =3D 0.0f;
    matrix.m[3][3] =3D 1.0f;
    IDirect3DDevice9_SetTransform(device, D3DTS_WORLD, &matrix);
    IDirect3DDevice9_SetTransform(device, D3DTS_VIEW, &matrix);


   /* Reset our current scale mode */
    SDL_memset(data->scaleMode, 0xFF, sizeof(data->scaleMode));


   /* Start the render with beginScene */
    data->beginScene =3D SDL_TRUE;
}

r * GL_CreateRenderer(SDL_Window * window, Uint32 flags)
{
    SDL_Renderer *renderer;

    SDL_GL_GetAttribute(SDL_GL_CONTEXT_PROFILE_MASK, &profile_mask);
    SDL_GL_GetAttribute(SDL_GL_CONTEXT_MAJOR_VERSION, &major);
    SDL_GL_GetAttribute(SDL_GL_CONTEXT_MINOR_VERSION, &minor);
   =20
    window_flags =3D SDL_GetWindowFlags(window);
    if (!(window_flags & SDL_WINDOW_OPENGL) ||
        profile_mask =3D=3D SDL_GL_CONTEXT_PROFILE_ES || major !=3D RENDERE=
R_CONTEXT_MAJOR || minor !=3D RENDERER_CONTEXT_MINOR) {
       =20
        SDL_GL_SetAttribute(SDL_GL_CONTEXT_PROFILE_MASK, 0);
        SDL_GL_SetAttribute(SDL_GL_CONTEXT_MAJOR_VERSION, RENDERER_CONTEXT_=
MAJOR);
        SDL_GL_SetAttribute(SDL_GL_CONTEXT_MINOR_VERSION, RENDERER_CONTEXT_=
MINOR);


        if (SDL_RecreateWindow(window, window_flags | SDL_WINDOW_OPENGL) &l=
t; 0) {
           /* Uh oh, better try to put it back... */
            SDL_GL_SetAttribute(SDL_GL_CONTEXT_PROFILE_MASK, profile_mask);
            SDL_GL_SetAttribute(SDL_GL_CONTEXT_MAJOR_VERSION, major);
            SDL_GL_SetAttribute(SDL_GL_CONTEXT_MINOR_VERSION, minor);
            SDL_RecreateWindow(window, window_flags);
            return NULL;
        }
    }


    renderer =3D (SDL_Renderer *) SDL_calloc(1, sizeof(*renderer));
    if (!renderer) {
        SDL_OutOfMemory();
        return NULL;
    }


    data =3D (GL_RenderData *) SDL_calloc(1, sizeof(*data));
    if (!data) {
        GL_DestroyRenderer(renderer);
        SDL_OutOfMemory();
        return NULL;
    }


    renderer->WindowEvent =3D GL_WindowEvent;
    renderer->GetOutputSize =3D GL_GetOutputSize;
    renderer->CreateTexture =3D GL_CreateTexture;
    renderer->UpdateTexture =3D GL_UpdateTexture;
    renderer->UpdateTextureYUV =3D GL_UpdateTextureYUV;
    renderer->LockTexture =3D GL_LockTexture;
    renderer->UnlockTexture =3D GL_UnlockTexture;
    renderer->SetRenderTarget =3D GL_SetRenderTarget;
    renderer->UpdateViewport =3D GL_UpdateViewport;
    renderer->UpdateClipRect =3D GL_UpdateClipRect;
    renderer->RenderClear =3D GL_RenderClear;
    renderer->RenderDrawPoints =3D GL_RenderDrawPoints;
    renderer->RenderDrawLines =3D GL_RenderDrawLines;
    renderer->RenderFillRects =3D GL_RenderFillRects;
    renderer->RenderCopy =3D GL_RenderCopy;
    renderer->RenderCopyEx =3D GL_RenderCopyEx;
    renderer->RenderReadPixels =3D GL_RenderReadPixels;
    renderer->RenderPresent =3D GL_RenderPresent;

RGETTEXTURE);
    renderer->driverdata =3D data;
    renderer->window =3D window;


    data->context =3D SDL_GL_CreateContext(window);
    if (!data->context) {
        GL_DestroyRenderer(renderer);
        return NULL;
    }
    if (SDL_GL_MakeCurrent(window, data->context) < 0) {
        GL_DestroyRenderer(renderer);
        return NULL;
    }


    if (GL_LoadFunctions(data) < 0) {
        GL_DestroyRenderer(renderer);
        return NULL;
    }


#ifdef __MACOSX__
   /* Enable multi-threaded rendering */
   /* Disabled until Ryan finishes his VBO/PBO code...
       CGLEnable(CGLGetCurrentContext(), kCGLCEMPEngine);
     */
#endif


    if (flags & SDL_RENDERER_PRESENTVSYNC) {
        SDL_GL_SetSwapInterval(1);
    } else {
        SDL_GL_SetSwapInterval(0);
    }

        renderer->info.flags |=3D SDL_RENDERER_PRESENTVSYNC;
    }


   /* Check for debug output support */
    if (SDL_GL_GetAttribute(SDL_GL_CONTEXT_FLAGS, &value) =3D=3D 0 &=
;&
        (value & SDL_GL_CONTEXT_DEBUG_FLAG)) {
        data->debug_enabled =3D SDL_TRUE;
    }
    if (data->debug_enabled && SDL_GL_ExtensionSupported("GL_ARB=
_debug_output")) {
        PFNGLDEBUGMESSAGECALLBACKARBPROC glDebugMessageCallbackARBFunc =3D =
(PFNGLDEBUGMESSAGECALLBACKARBPROC) SDL_GL_GetProcAddress("glDebugMessageCal=
lbackARB");


        data->GL_ARB_debug_output_supported =3D SDL_TRUE;
        data->glGetPointerv(GL_DEBUG_CALLBACK_FUNCTION_ARB, (GLvoid **)&=
amp;data->next_error_callback);
        data->glGetPointerv(GL_DEBUG_CALLBACK_USER_PARAM_ARB, &data-=
>next_error_userparam);
        glDebugMessageCallbackARBFunc(GL_HandleDebugMessage, renderer);


       /* Make sure our callback is called when errors actually happen */
        data->glEnable(GL_DEBUG_OUTPUT_SYNCHRONOUS_ARB);
    }


    if (SDL_GL_ExtensionSupported("GL_ARB_texture_rectangle")
        || SDL_GL_ExtensionSupported("GL_EXT_texture_rectangle")) {
        data->GL_ARB_texture_rectangle_supported =3D SDL_TRUE;
        data->glGetIntegerv(GL_MAX_RECTANGLE_TEXTURE_SIZE_ARB, &valu=
e);
        renderer->info.max_texture_width =3D value;
        renderer->info.max_texture_height =3D value;
    } else {
        data->glGetIntegerv(GL_MAX_TEXTURE_SIZE, &value);
        renderer->info.max_texture_width =3D value;
        renderer->info.max_texture_height =3D value;
    }


   /* Check for multitexture support */
    if (SDL_GL_ExtensionSupported("GL_ARB_multitexture")) {
        data->glActiveTextureARB =3D (PFNGLACTIVETEXTUREARBPROC) SDL_GL_=
GetProcAddress("glActiveTextureARB");
        if (data->glActiveTextureARB) {
            data->GL_ARB_multitexture_supported =3D SDL_TRUE;
            data->glGetIntegerv(GL_MAX_TEXTURE_UNITS_ARB, &data->=
num_texture_units);
        }
    }


   /* Check for shader support */
    hint =3D SDL_GetHint(SDL_HINT_RENDER_OPENGL_SHADERS);
    if (!hint || *hint !=3D '0') {
        data->shaders =3D GL_CreateShaderContext();
    }
    SDL_LogInfo(SDL_LOG_CATEGORY_RENDER, "OpenGL shaders: %s",
                data->shaders ? "ENABLED" : "DISABLED");


   /* We support YV12 textures using 3 textures and a shader */
    if (data->shaders && data->num_texture_units >=3D 3) {
        renderer->info.texture_formats[renderer->info.num_texture_for=
mats++] =3D SDL_PIXELFORMAT_YV12;
        renderer->info.texture_formats[renderer->info.num_texture_for=
mats++] =3D SDL_PIXELFORMAT_IYUV;
    }


#ifdef __MACOSX__
    renderer->info.texture_formats[renderer->info.num_texture_formats=
++] =3D SDL_PIXELFORMAT_UYVY;
#endif


    if (SDL_GL_ExtensionSupported("GL_EXT_framebuffer_object")) {
        data->GL_EXT_framebuffer_object_supported =3D SDL_TRUE;
        data->glGenFramebuffersEXT =3D (PFNGLGENFRAMEBUFFERSEXTPROC)
            SDL_GL_GetProcAddress("glGenFramebuffersEXT");
        data->glDeleteFramebuffersEXT =3D (PFNGLDELETEFRAMEBUFFERSEXTPRO=
C)

            SDL_GL_GetProcAddress("glBindFramebufferEXT");

USEXTPROC)

        renderer->info.flags |=3D SDL_RENDERER_TARGETTEXTURE;
    }
    data->framebuffers =3D NULL;


   /* Set up parameters for rendering */
    GL_ResetState(renderer);


    return renderer;

GL_ShaderContext * GL_CreateShaderContext()
{

        ctx->glUniform1fARB =3D (PFNGLUNIFORM1FARBPROC) SDL_GL_GetProcAd=
dress("glUniform1fARB");
        ctx->glUseProgramObjectARB =3D (PFNGLUSEPROGRAMOBJECTARBPROC) SD=
L_GL_GetProcAddress("glUseProgramObjectARB");
        if (ctx->glGetError &&
            ctx->glAttachObjectARB &&
            ctx->glCompileShaderARB &&
            ctx->glCreateProgramObjectARB &&
            ctx->glCreateShaderObjectARB &&
            ctx->glDeleteObjectARB &&
            ctx->glGetInfoLogARB &&
            ctx->glGetObjectParameterivARB &&
            ctx->glGetUniformLocationARB &&
            ctx->glLinkProgramARB &&
            ctx->glShaderSourceARB &&
            ctx->glUniform1iARB &&
            ctx->glUniform1fARB &&
            ctx->glUseProgramObjectARB) {
            shaders_supported =3D SDL_TRUE;
        }
    }


    if (!shaders_supported) {
        SDL_free(ctx);
        return NULL;
    }


   /* Compile all the shaders */
    for (i =3D 0; i < NUM_SHADERS; ++i) {
        if (!CompileShaderProgram(ctx, i, &ctx->shaders[i])) {
            GL_DestroyShaderContext(ctx);
            return NULL;
        }
    }


   /* We're done! */
    return ctx;
}

The code mainly finished two steps:
the first step, = initialization GL_ShaderContext. GL_ShaderContext included Shader = used in various aspects of the interface functions of OpenGL. GL_ShaderCont= ext example, the following is defined.
struct GL_ShaderContext
{
    GLenum (*glGetError)(void);


    PFNGLATTACHOBJECTARBPROC glAttachObjectARB;
    PFNGLCOMPILESHADERARBPROC glCompileShaderARB;
    PFNGLCREATEPROGRAMOBJECTARBPROC glCreateProgramObjectARB;
    PFNGLCREATESHADEROBJECTARBPROC glCreateShaderObjectARB;
    PFNGLDELETEOBJECTARBPROC glDeleteObjectARB;
    PFNGLGETINFOLOGARBPROC glGetInfoLogARB;
    PFNGLGETOBJECTPARAMETERIVARBPROC glGetObjectParameterivARB;
    PFNGLGETUNIFORMLOCATIONARBPROC glGetUniformLocationARB;
    PFNGLLINKPROGRAMARBPROC glLinkProgramARB;
    PFNGLSHADERSOURCEARBPROC glShaderSourceARB;
    PFNGLUNIFORM1IARBPROC glUniform1iARB;
    PFNGLUNIFORM1FARBPROC glUniform1fARB;
    PFNGLUSEPROGRAMOBJECTARBPROC glUseProgramObjectARB;


    SDL_bool GL_ARB_texture_rectangle_supported;


    GL_ShaderData shaders[NUM_SHADERS];
};

This definition will give people see the structure of a very co= nfusing feeling.

Just ignore those strings of large capital letters, just= to know that this structure is a "collection" interface function on it.

From the name of the function, we can see that there Shader compilation= of glCreateShaderObject (), glShaderSource (), glCompileShader () and so o= n; and compiling Program of glCreateProgramObject (). glAttachObject (), gl= LinkProgram (), glUseProgramObject () and so on.
GL_CreateShaderContext= () function creates a GL_ShaderContext and among the interface functions w= ere assigned.

The second step, Shader compiler program. This function is completed in CompileShaderProgram () function.

CompileShaderProgram () function code, for example, see below.

static SD= L_bool CompileShaderProgram(GL_ShaderContext *ctx, int index, GL_ShaderData= *data) { const int num_tmus_bound =3D 4; const char *vert_defines =3D ""; const char *frag_defines =3D ""; int i; GLint location; if (index =3D=3D SHADER_NONE) { return SDL_TRUE; } ctx->glGetError(); /* Make sure we use the correct sampler type for our texture type */ if (ctx->GL_ARB_texture_rectangle_supported) { frag_defines =3D "#define sampler2D sampler2DRect\n" "#define texture2D texture2DRect\n"; } /* Create one program object to rule them all */ data->program =3D ctx->glCreateProgramObjectARB(); /* Create the vertex shader */ data->vert_shader =3D ctx->glCreateShaderObjectARB(GL_VERTEX_SHAD= ER_ARB); if (!CompileShader(ctx, data->vert_shader, vert_defines, shader_sour= ce[index][0])) { return SDL_FALSE; } /* Create the fragment shader */ data->frag_shader =3D ctx->glCreateShaderObjectARB(GL_FRAGMENT_SH= ADER_ARB); if (!CompileShader(ctx, data->frag_shader, frag_defines, shader_sour= ce[index][1])) { return SDL_FALSE; } /* ... and in the darkness bind them */ ctx->glAttachObjectARB(data->program, data->vert_shader); ctx->glAttachObjectARB(data->program, data->frag_shader); ctx->glLinkProgramARB(data->program); /* Set up some uniform variables */ ctx->glUseProgramObjectARB(data->program); for (i =3D 0; i < num_tmus_bound; ++i) { char tex_name[10]; SDL_snprintf(tex_name, SDL_arraysize(tex_name), "tex%d", i); location =3D ctx->glGetUniformLocationARB(data->program, tex_= name); if (location >=3D 0) { ctx->glUniform1iARB(location, i); } } ctx->glUseProgramObjectARB(0); return (ctx->glGetError() =3D=3D GL_NO_ERROR); }

As can be seen from the code. This function calls for each fu= nction GL_ShaderContext initialization and Shader Program. Process-related = initialization not elaborate, you can refer to the relevant articles.

In= this function, called CompileShader () designed to initialize Shader.

Th= is function is called twice, respectively, is used to initialize vertex sha= der and fragment shader.

CompileShader (), for example, the follo= wing code.

static SDL_bool CompileShader(GL_ShaderContext *ctx, GLhandleARB s=
hader, const char *defines, const char *source)
{
    GLint status;
    const char *sources[2];


    sources[0] =3D defines;
    sources[1] =3D source;


    ctx->glShaderSourceARB(shader, SDL_arraysize(sources), sources, NULL=
);
    ctx->glCompileShaderARB(shader);
    ctx->glGetObjectParameterivARB(shader, GL_OBJECT_COMPILE_STATUS_ARB,=
 &status);
    if (status =3D=3D 0) {
        GLint length;
        char *info;


        ctx->glGetObjectParameterivARB(shader, GL_OBJECT_INFO_LOG_LENGTH=
_ARB, &length);
        info =3D SDL_stack_alloc(char, length+1);
        ctx->glGetInfoLogARB(shader, length, NULL, info);
        SDL_LogError(SDL_LOG_CATEGORY_RENDER,
            "Failed to compile shader:\n%s%s\n%s", defines, source, info);
#ifdef DEBUG_SHADERS
        fprintf(stderr,
            "Failed to compile shader:\n%s%s\n%s", defines, source, info);
#endif
        SDL_stack_free(info);


        return SDL_FALSE;
    } else {
        return SDL_TRUE;
    }
}

As can be seen from the code, the function call glShaderSource (= ). glCompileShader (). glGetObjectParameteriv () This function initializes = a few Shader.
Shader code name for the char type in a two-dimensional a= rray shader_source's. Source code for example, see.

Each array element re= presents a code Shader, Shader each code consists of two parts: vertex shad= er codes (corresponding to the element [0]) and a fragment shader codes (co= rresponding element [1]).

/*
 * NOTE: Always use sampler2D, etc here. We'll #define them to the
 *  texture_rectangle versions if we choose to use that extension.
 */
static const char *shader_source[NUM_SHADERS][2] =3D
{
   /* SHADER_NONE */
    { NULL, NULL },


   /* SHADER_SOLID */
    {
       /* vertex shader */
"varying vec4 v_color;\n"
"\n"
"void main()\n"
"{\n"
"    gl_Position =3D gl_ModelViewProjectionMatrix * gl_Vertex;\n"
"    v_color =3D gl_Color;\n"
"}",
       /* fragment shader */
"varying vec4 v_color;\n"
"\n"
"void main()\n"
"{\n"
"    gl_FragColor =3D v_color;\n"
"}"
    },


   /* SHADER_RGB */
    {
       /* vertex shader */
"varying vec4 v_color;\n"
"varying vec2 v_texCoord;\n"
"\n"
"void main()\n"
"{\n"
"    gl_Position =3D gl_ModelViewProjectionMatrix * gl_Vertex;\n"
"    v_color =3D gl_Color;\n"
"    v_texCoord =3D vec2(gl_MultiTexCoord0);\n"
"}",
       /* fragment shader */
"varying vec4 v_color;\n"
"varying vec2 v_texCoord;\n"
"uniform sampler2D tex0;\n"
"\n"
"void main()\n"
"{\n"
"    gl_FragColor =3D texture2D(tex0, v_texCoord) * v_color;\n"
"}"
    },


   /* SHADER_YV12 */
    {
       /* vertex shader */
"varying vec4 v_color;\n"
"varying vec2 v_texCoord;\n"
"\n"
"void main()\n"
"{\n"
"    gl_Position =3D gl_ModelViewProjectionMatrix * gl_Vertex;\n"
"    v_color =3D gl_Color;\n"
"    v_texCoord =3D vec2(gl_MultiTexCoord0);\n"
"}",
       /* fragment shader */
"varying vec4 v_color;\n"
"varying vec2 v_texCoord;\n"
"uniform sampler2D tex0;//Y\n"
"uniform sampler2D tex1;//U\n"
"uniform sampler2D tex2;//V\n"
"\n"
"//YUV offset\n"
"const vec3 offset =3D vec3(-0.0625, -0.5, -0.5);\n"
"\n"
"//RGB coefficients\n"
"const vec3 Rcoeff =3D vec3(1.164,  0.000,  1.596);\n"
"const vec3 Gcoeff =3D vec3(1.164, -0.391, -0.813);\n"
"const vec3 Bcoeff =3D vec3(1.164,  2.018,  0.000);\n"
"\n"
"void main()\n"
"{\n"
"    vec2 tcoord;\n"
"    vec3 yuv, rgb;\n"
"\n"
"   //Get the Y value\n"
"    tcoord =3D v_texCoord;\n"
"    yuv.x =3D texture2D(tex0, tcoord).r;\n"
"\n"
"   //Get the U and V values\n"
"    tcoord *=3D 0.5;\n"
"    yuv.y =3D texture2D(tex1, tcoord).r;\n"
"    yuv.z =3D texture2D(tex2, tcoord).r;\n"
"\n"
"   //Do the color transform\n"
"    yuv +=3D offset;\n"
"    rgb.r =3D dot(yuv, Rcoeff);\n"
"    rgb.g =3D dot(yuv, Gcoeff);\n"
"    rgb.b =3D dot(yuv, Bcoeff);\n"
"\n"
"   //That was easy. :)\n"
"    gl_FragColor =3D vec4(rgb, 1.0) * v_color;\n"
"}"
    },
};

Initialization code related to the OpenGL renderer interim anal= ysis here.

3.Software

Software renderer creating function is = SW_CreateRenderer (). This function is located render\software\SDL_render_s= w.c file. First look at its code.

SDL_Renderer * SW_CreateRenderer(SDL_Window=
 * window, Uint32 flags)
{
    SDL_Surface *surface;


    surface =3D SDL_GetWindowSurface(window);
    if (!surface) {
        return NULL;
    }
    return SW_CreateRendererForSurface(surface);
}

As can be seen from the code, SW_CreateRenderer () function call= to the 2: SDL_GetWindowSurface () and SW_CreateRendererForSurface (). SDL_= GetWindowSurface () is used to create a Surface; SW_CreateRendererForSurfac= e () based on Surface create a Renderer.
The following are a look at th= e code for these two functions.
SDL_GetWindowSurface () code for exampl= e, see (in the video\SDL_video.c).
SDL_Surface * SDL_GetWindowSurface(SDL_Win=
dow * window)
{
    CHECK_WINDOW_MAGIC(window, NULL);


    if (!window->surface_valid) {
        if (window->surface) {
            window->surface->flags &=3D ~SDL_DONTFREE;
            SDL_FreeSurface(window->surface);
        }
        window->surface =3D SDL_CreateWindowFramebuffer(window);
        if (window->surface) {
            window->surface_valid =3D SDL_TRUE;
            window->surface->flags |=3D SDL_DONTFREE;
        }
    }
    return window->surface;
}

Which calls a function SDL_CreateWindowFramebuffer (). Look at t= he code for this function.
static SDL_Surface * SDL_CreateWindowFramebuffer=
(SDL_Window * window)
{
    Uint32 format;
    void *pixels;
    int pitch;
    int bpp;
    Uint32 Rmask, Gmask, Bmask, Amask;


    if (!_this->CreateWindowFramebuffer || !_this->UpdateWindowFrameb=
uffer) {
        return NULL;
    }


    if (_this->CreateWindowFramebuffer(_this, window, &format, &=
pixels, &pitch) < 0) {
        return NULL;
    }


    if (!SDL_PixelFormatEnumToMasks(format, &bpp, &Rmask, &Gmas=
k, &Bmask, &Amask)) {
        return NULL;
    }


    return SDL_CreateRGBSurfaceFrom(pixels, window->w, window->h, bpp=
, pitch, Rmask, Gmask, Bmask, Amask);
}

This function calls a function CreateWindowFramebuffer SDL_Vi= deoDevice in ().

Our "Windows video driver" for example, look at the = code () in CreateWindowFramebuffer. In "Windows video driver", the correspo= nding function CreateWindowFramebuffer () is WIN_CreateWindowFramebuffer ()= .

The following look at the code for this function.

int WIN_CreateWindo=
wFramebuffer(_THIS, SDL_Window * window, Uint32 * format, void ** pixels, i=
nt *pitch)
{
    SDL_WindowData *data =3D (SDL_WindowData *) window->driverdata;
    size_t size;
    LPBITMAPINFO info;
    HBITMAP hbm;


   /* Free the old framebuffer surface */
    if (data->mdc) {
        DeleteDC(data->mdc);
    }
    if (data->hbm) {
        DeleteObject(data->hbm);
    }


   /* Find out the format of the screen */
    size =3D sizeof(BITMAPINFOHEADER) + 256 * sizeof (RGBQUAD);
    info =3D (LPBITMAPINFO)SDL_stack_alloc(Uint8, size);


    SDL_memset(info, 0, size);
    info->bmiHeader.biSize =3D sizeof(BITMAPINFOHEADER);


   /* The second call to GetDIBits() fills in the bitfields */
    hbm =3D CreateCompatibleBitmap(data->hdc, 1, 1);
    GetDIBits(data->hdc, hbm, 0, 0, NULL, info, DIB_RGB_COLORS);
    GetDIBits(data->hdc, hbm, 0, 0, NULL, info, DIB_RGB_COLORS);
    DeleteObject(hbm);


    *format =3D SDL_PIXELFORMAT_UNKNOWN;
    if (info->bmiHeader.biCompression =3D=3D BI_BITFIELDS) {
        int bpp;
        Uint32 *masks;


        bpp =3D info->bmiHeader.biPlanes * info->bmiHeader.biBitCount=
;
        masks =3D (Uint32*)((Uint8*)info + info->bmiHeader.biSize);
        *format =3D SDL_MasksToPixelFormatEnum(bpp, masks[0], masks[1], mas=
ks[2], 0);
    }
    if (*format =3D=3D SDL_PIXELFORMAT_UNKNOWN)
    {
       /* We'll use RGB format for now */
        *format =3D SDL_PIXELFORMAT_RGB888;


       /* Create a new one */
        SDL_memset(info, 0, size);
        info->bmiHeader.biSize =3D sizeof(BITMAPINFOHEADER);
        info->bmiHeader.biPlanes =3D 1;
        info->bmiHeader.biBitCount =3D 32;
        info->bmiHeader.biCompression =3D BI_RGB;
    }


   /* Fill in the size information */
    *pitch =3D (((window->w * SDL_BYTESPERPIXEL(*format)) + 3) & ~3)=
;
    info->bmiHeader.biWidth =3D window->w;
    info->bmiHeader.biHeight =3D -window->h; /* negative for topdown =
bitmap */
    info->bmiHeader.biSizeImage =3D window->h * (*pitch);


    data->mdc =3D CreateCompatibleDC(data->hdc);
    data->hbm =3D CreateDIBSection(data->hdc, info, DIB_RGB_COLORS, p=
ixels, NULL, 0);
    SDL_stack_free(info);


    if (!data->hbm) {
        return WIN_SetError("Unable to create DIB");
    }
    SelectObject(data->mdc, data->hbm);


    return 0;
}

As can be seen from the code, the function calls the Win32 API f= unction CreateCompatibleBitmap (), CreateCompatibleDC () method creates a s= eries of "Surface".



SDL_GetWindowSurface () function to this anal= ysis is completed, and now back to look at SW_CreateRenderer () is also a f= unction SW_CreateRendererForSurface ().

For example, the following co= de for this function.

SDL_Renderer * SW_CreateRendererForSurface(SDL_Surface =
* surface)
{
    SDL_Renderer *renderer;
    SW_RenderData *data;


    if (!surface) {
        SDL_SetError("Can't create renderer for NULL surface");
        return NULL;
    }


    renderer =3D (SDL_Renderer *) SDL_calloc(1, sizeof(*renderer));
    if (!renderer) {
        SDL_OutOfMemory();
        return NULL;
    }


    data =3D (SW_RenderData *) SDL_calloc(1, sizeof(*data));
    if (!data) {
        SW_DestroyRenderer(renderer);
        SDL_OutOfMemory();
        return NULL;
    }
    data->surface =3D surface;


    renderer->WindowEvent =3D SW_WindowEvent;
    renderer->GetOutputSize =3D SW_GetOutputSize;
    renderer->CreateTexture =3D SW_CreateTexture;
    renderer->SetTextureColorMod =3D SW_SetTextureColorMod;
    renderer->SetTextureAlphaMod =3D SW_SetTextureAlphaMod;
    renderer->SetTextureBlendMode =3D SW_SetTextureBlendMode;
    renderer->UpdateTexture =3D SW_UpdateTexture;
    renderer->LockTexture =3D SW_LockTexture;
    renderer->UnlockTexture =3D SW_UnlockTexture;
    renderer->SetRenderTarget =3D SW_SetRenderTarget;
    renderer->UpdateViewport =3D SW_UpdateViewport;
    renderer->UpdateClipRect =3D SW_UpdateClipRect;
    renderer->RenderClear =3D SW_RenderClear;
    renderer->RenderDrawPoints =3D SW_RenderDrawPoints;
    renderer->RenderDrawLines =3D SW_RenderDrawLines;
    renderer->RenderFillRects =3D SW_RenderFillRects;
    renderer->RenderCopy =3D SW_RenderCopy;
    renderer->RenderCopyEx =3D SW_RenderCopyEx;
    renderer->RenderReadPixels =3D SW_RenderReadPixels;
    renderer->RenderPresent =3D SW_RenderPresent;
    renderer->DestroyTexture =3D SW_DestroyTexture;
    renderer->DestroyRenderer =3D SW_DestroyRenderer;
    renderer->info =3D SW_RenderDriver.info;
    renderer->driverdata =3D data;


    SW_ActivateRenderer(renderer);


    return renderer;
}

Like the previous function, the function assignment SDL_Renderer= finished structural body function pointer.
